## üîç Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### üéØ Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 40 page(s) - 40 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [landmark-unique](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-unique?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: Landmarks should have a unique role or role/label/title (i.e. accessible name) combination

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<nav class="widgetGraphicLinksNav" aria-label="Graphic links">
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
#graphicLinkWidgetc26a0721-77ca-4ae4-8b81-30760b07e12a > .cpGrid2.widgetBody.cpGrid > .widgetGraphicLinksNav[aria-label="Graphic links"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('#graphicLinkWidgetc26a0721-77ca-4ae4-8b81-30760b07e12a > .cpGrid2.widgetBody.cpGrid > .widgetGraphicLinksNav[aria-label="Graphic links"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://www.cityofdenton.com/
- https://daytonohio.gov/
- https://www.elizabethnj.org/
- http://www.hampton.gov/
- https://www.sterlingheights.gov/
- *...and 35 more page(s)*

**Scanner**: axe
**Rule**: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate
**Issue**: All page content should be contained by landmarks

#### Pattern 3: Affects 23 page(s) - 24 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**Issue**: Target has insufficient size

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<a class="widgetDesc widgetQuickLinksLink" href="/" target="_self">Home</a>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/a[@class="widgetDesc widgetQuickLinksLink"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/a[@class="widgetDesc widgetQuickLinksLink"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://www.cityofdenton.com/

#### Rule: [SIA-R11: Button elements have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r11)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="/CivicAlerts.aspx?AID=1226" target="_self">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="/CivicAlerts.aspx?AID=1229" target="_self">Novartis to Build New Radioligand Therapy Site in ...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

- XPath: `/a[@id="newsFlashReadOn1229"]`

**Failure 3:**

- HTML: `<a id="newsFlashReadOn1226" href="/CivicAlerts.aspx?AID=1226" target="_self" class="readOn" aria-labelledby="newsFlashItemHeader1226 newsFlashReadOn1226">Read on...</a>`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The link does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<a href="index.php">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a`

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="newslist.php" target="_self" class="footer-list-link">News</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="footer-list-link"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://twitter.com/cityofsparks" target="_blank" class="social-media-link" rel="noopener">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="social-media-link"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R12: Links have an accessible name](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r12)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The button does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<button class="sr-only" />`
- XPath: `/button[@class="sr-only"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The button does not have an accessible name
- HTML: `<button type="button" data-controls="prev" tabindex="-1" aria-controls="quick-links">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button`

#### Rule: [SIA-R17](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r17)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<div class="qlink-item tns-item tns-slide-cloned" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="qlink-item tns-item tns-slide-cloned"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<div class="qlink-item tns-item" id="quick-links-item1" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="quick-links-item1"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<div class="nlink-item tns-item tns-slide-cloned" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@class="nlink-item tns-item tns-slide-cloned"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<div class="nlink-item tns-item" id="news-links-item3" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="news-links-item3"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element is either tabbable or has tabbable descendants
- HTML: `<div class="nlink-item tns-item" id="news-links-item4" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1">...</div>`
- XPath: `/div[@id="news-links-item4"]`

- XPath: `/div[@id="goog-gt-tt"]`

- HTML: `<a href="https://www.springfi..." target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="carousel-item active" data-bs-interval="7000" role="img" aria-label="2026 Grass Cutting/B..." style="background-image: ur...">`
- XPath: `.active`

#### Rule: [landmark-banner-is-top-level](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-banner-is-top-level?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Banner landmark should not be contained in another landmark
- HTML: `<header role="banner" aria-label="Site header">`
- XPath: `header`

#### Rule: [landmark-main-is-top-level](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/landmark-main-is-top-level?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Main landmark should not be contained in another landmark
- HTML: `<main id="main-content" role="main" tabindex="-1" aria-label="Main content">`
- XPath: `main[aria-label="Main content"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Main landmark should not be contained in another landmark
- HTML: `<main id="main-content" role="main" aria-label="Main content - City of Springfield">`
- XPath: `main[aria-label="Main content"] > main`

**Impact**: moderate

- HTML: `<main id="main-content" role="main" tabindex="-1" aria-label="Main content">`
- XPath: `main[aria-label="Main content"]`

**Impact**: serious

- XPath: `.navbar-nav[aria-label="Site navigation menu"]:nth-child(1)`
